  \Gscale@div\@tempa{\textheight}{\dimexpr\ht\pandoc@box+\dp\pandoc@box\relax}%
  \Gscale@div\@tempb{\linewidth}{\wd\pandoc@box}%
  \ifdim\@tempb\p@<\@tempa\p@\let\@tempa\@tempb\fi% select the smaller of both
  \ifdim\@tempa\p@<\p@\scalebox{\@tempa}{\usebox\pandoc@box}%
  \else\usebox{\pandoc@box}%
  \fi%

\section{Cleaning:}\label{cleaning}

Find the groups of demographics dataset:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{demographics }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(Reason) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{count =} \FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{())}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
# A tibble: 5 x 2
  Reason        count
  <chr>         <int>
1 Diaper-Change   500
2 Fussy           500
3 Hungry          500
4 Pain            500
5 Tired           500
\end{verbatim}

I see some no email and no gender and no age. clean the demographics
data

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# demographics \textless{}{-} demographics \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   filter(ID != \textquotesingle{}NO{-}EMAIL\textquotesingle{}, Age != \textquotesingle{}NO{-}AGE\textquotesingle{}, Gender != \textquotesingle{}NO{-}GENDER\textquotesingle{})}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# demographics \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   group\_by(Reason) \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   summarise(count = n())}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{full\_data\_odd }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(ParentFile) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{count =} \FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{())}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
# A tibble: 5 x 2
  ParentFile             count
  <chr>                  <int>
1 gemaps_part_diaper.csv   250
2 gemaps_part_fussy.csv    250
3 gemaps_part_hungry.csv   250
4 gemaps_part_pain.csv     250
5 gemaps_part_tired.csv    250
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{demographics }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(Reason) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{count =} \FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{())}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
# A tibble: 5 x 2
  Reason        count
  <chr>         <int>
1 Diaper-Change   500
2 Fussy           500
3 Hungry          500
4 Pain            500
5 Tired           500
\end{verbatim}

Join the two datasets:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# \# Filter out email and no email separately }
\CommentTok{\# demographics\_no\_em \textless{}{-} demographics \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   filter(ID == "NO{-}EMAIL")}
\CommentTok{\# demographics\_em \textless{}{-} demographics \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   filter(ID != "NO{-}EMAIL")}

\CommentTok{\# full\_data\_no\_em \textless{}{-} full\_data\_odd \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   filter(str\_detect(Filename, "\^{}NO{-}EMAIL"))}
\CommentTok{\# full\_data\_em \textless{}{-} full\_data\_odd \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   filter(!str\_detect(Filename, "\^{}NO{-}EMAIL"))}

\CommentTok{\# For the email, join by ID}
\NormalTok{full\_data\_mod }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ full\_data\_odd }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\#mutate(ID = str\_split(Filename, "\_")[1]) \%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{separate}\NormalTok{(Filename, }\AttributeTok{into =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Comp"}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{relocate}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Comp"}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{8}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{.before =}\NormalTok{ ParentFile) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{rename}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{ID =} \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Comp1}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{Reason =}\NormalTok{ Comp2, }\AttributeTok{Age =}\NormalTok{ Comp3, }\AttributeTok{Gender =}\NormalTok{ Comp4, }\AttributeTok{Date =}\NormalTok{ Comp5, }\AttributeTok{Sample =}\NormalTok{ Comp6) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Comp7, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Comp8)}

\CommentTok{\# join\_em \textless{}{-} left\_join(full\_data\_em, demographics\_em)}

\CommentTok{\# For the no email, join by the sample ID plus date}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# write\_csv(full\_data\_mod, "full\_data\_mod.csv")}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\subsection{Chi-Square}\label{chi-square}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# chi square test between gender and reason}
\FunctionTok{chisq.test}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(demographics}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Gender, demographics}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
Warning in stats::chisq.test(x, y, ...): Chi-squared approximation may be
incorrect
\end{verbatim}

\begin{verbatim}

    Pearson's Chi-squared test

data:  table(demographics$Gender, demographics$Reason)
X-squared = 27.608, df = 12, p-value = 0.00631
\end{verbatim}

\subsection{ANOVA w/ removed missing
ages}\label{anova-w-removed-missing-ages}

\begin{Shaded}

\CommentTok{\# anova between age and reason}
\CommentTok{\# convert missing ages to NA}
\NormalTok{demographics}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Age[demographics}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Age }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"NO{-}AGE"}\NormalTok{] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{NA}
\NormalTok{demographics}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Age }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(demographics}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Age)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\end{verbatim}

\subsection{Scree Plot by Cry Acoustics
Dimensions}\label{scree-plot-by-cry-acoustics-dimensions}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# see how the acoustic feastures measure}
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(factoextra)}
\CommentTok{\# get numeric only}
\NormalTok{acoustic\_features }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ full\_data\_odd }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{where}\NormalTok{(is.numeric)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{na.omit}\NormalTok{()  }

\CommentTok{\#scale for scree plot}
\NormalTok{scaled\_features }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{scale}\NormalTok{(acoustic\_features)}
\NormalTok{pca }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{prcomp}\NormalTok{(scaled\_features, }\AttributeTok{center =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{scale. =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# plot the scree plot}
\FunctionTok{fviz\_eig}\NormalTok{(pca, }\AttributeTok{addlabels =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{barfill =} \StringTok{"steelblue"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
  \FunctionTok{labs}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{title =} \StringTok{"Scree Plot"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\section{Question 2: Unsupervised
learning}\label{question-2-unsupervised-learning}

\subsubsection{K-means Clustering Attempt
1}\label{k-means-clustering-attempt-1}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read.csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"./full\_data\_cleaned\_without\_nas.csv"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{header=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\#loading data}
\NormalTok{data2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ data}
\NormalTok{data2}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason) }\CommentTok{\# factor data}

\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{333}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# set up training data}
\NormalTok{trainIndex }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{createDataPartition}\NormalTok{(data2}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason, }\AttributeTok{p =} \FloatTok{0.8}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{list =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{trainData }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ data2[trainIndex, ]}
\NormalTok{testData }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ data2[}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{trainIndex, ]}

\NormalTok{ctrl }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{trainControl}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{method =} \StringTok{"cv"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{number =} \DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{verboseIter =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# tart fresh}
\NormalTok{data5 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ data}

\CommentTok{\# only acoustic data}
\NormalTok{acoustic\_numeric }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ data5 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{where}\NormalTok{(is.numeric))}

\CommentTok{\# Scale the features}
\NormalTok{acoustic\_scaled }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{scale}\NormalTok{(acoustic\_numeric)}

\CommentTok{\#k{-}means clustering (k=5)}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{123}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{5}
\NormalTok{kmeans\_res }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{kmeans}\NormalTok{(acoustic\_scaled, }\AttributeTok{centers =}\NormalTok{ k, }\AttributeTok{nstart =} \DecValTok{25}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# add cluster labels to data5}
\NormalTok{data5}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Cluster }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(kmeans\_res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster)}

\CommentTok{\#print results}
\FunctionTok{table}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{Cluster =}\NormalTok{ data5}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Cluster, }\AttributeTok{Reason =}\NormalTok{ data5}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
       Reason
Cluster Diaper-Change Fussy Hungry Pain Tired
      1            45    22     50   56    28
      2            45    34     76   47    61
      3            48    70     41   28    40
      4             9     8      5    7     7
      5            32    44      0   30    35
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{data5}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Cluster }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(data5}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Cluster)  }\CommentTok{\# facotr data}

\CommentTok{\#prepare dataset for classification}
\NormalTok{dataset\_for\_cluster\_pred }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ data5 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Reason, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Gender, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Age, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{newID, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Date, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Sample)  }\CommentTok{\# keep acoustic + Cluster}

\CommentTok{\# 10{-}fold cross{-}validation}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{123}\NormalTok{)}

\subsubsection{Spectral Clustering}\label{spectral-clustering}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# generate random data for clustering}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{605794011}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{k }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{5}

\CommentTok{\# extract the first two principal components}
\NormalTok{PC1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ pca\_result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x[, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{PC2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ pca\_result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x[, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{]}

\CommentTok{\# compute the similarity matrix}
\NormalTok{similarity\_matrix }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{exp}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\FunctionTok{dist}\NormalTok{(clust\_data)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# perform spectral decomposition}
\NormalTok{eigen\_result }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{eigen}\NormalTok{(similarity\_matrix)}

\CommentTok{\# extract the top{-}k eigenvectors}
\NormalTok{k\_eigenvectors }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ eigen\_result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{vectors[, }\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\NormalTok{k]}

\CommentTok{\# perform k{-}means clustering on the eigenvectors}
\NormalTok{cluster\_assignments }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{kmeans}\NormalTok{(k\_eigenvectors, }\AttributeTok{centers =}\NormalTok{ k)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{cluster}

\CommentTok{\# visualize clusters}
\NormalTok{cluster\_colors }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rainbow}\NormalTok{(k)}
\FunctionTok{plot}\NormalTok{(PC1, PC2, }\AttributeTok{col =}\NormalTok{ cluster\_colors[cluster\_assignments], }\AttributeTok{pch =} \DecValTok{19}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{cex =} \FloatTok{0.7}\NormalTok{,}
     \AttributeTok{main =} \StringTok{"Spectral Clustering with k{-}means"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{xlab =} \StringTok{"PC1"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{ylab =} \StringTok{"PC2"}\NormalTok{)}
\FunctionTok{legend}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"topright"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{legend =} \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Cluster"}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\SpecialCharTok{:}\NormalTok{k), }\AttributeTok{col =}\NormalTok{ cluster\_colors, }\AttributeTok{pch =} \DecValTok{19}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]

\subsubsection{Random Forest w/ mice
imputation}\label{random-forest-w-mice-imputation}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# create method vector for mice}
\NormalTok{methods }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{make.method}\NormalTok{(rf\_with\_nas)}
\NormalTok{rf\_with\_nas}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Gender[rf\_with\_nas}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Gender }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"MULT{-}REDCAP{-}GENDER"}\NormalTok{] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{NA}

\NormalTok{init }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{mice}\NormalTok{(rf\_with\_nas, }\AttributeTok{maxit =} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)  }
\NormalTok{methods }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ init}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{method                }
\NormalTok{methods[}\StringTok{"Reason"}\NormalTok{] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{""}
\NormalTok{methods[}\StringTok{"Gender"}\NormalTok{] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"logreg"}  \CommentTok{\# or "polyreg" if \textgreater{}2 levels}

\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]

\CommentTok{\# ensure target and gender are factors}

\NormalTok{data\_imputed}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Gender }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(data\_imputed}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Gender)}

\CommentTok{\# fit random forest model}

\CommentTok{\# predictions and evaluations of accuracy}

\subsubsection{XGBoost}\label{xgboost}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# ensure Reason is a factor}
\NormalTok{data\_imputed}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(data\_imputed}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason)}

\CommentTok{\# clean up class levels to be valid R variable names}
\FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(data\_imputed}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason) }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{make.names}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(data\_imputed}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason))}

\CommentTok{\# train/test split (optional if using cross{-}validation)}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{605794011}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{train\_index }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{createDataPartition}\NormalTok{(data\_imputed}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Reason, }\AttributeTok{p =} \FloatTok{0.8}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{list =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{train\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ data\_imputed[train\_index, ]}
\NormalTok{test\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ data\_imputed[}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{train\_index, ]}

\CommentTok{\# cross{-}validation setup}
\NormalTok{ctrl }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{trainControl}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{method =} \StringTok{"cv"}\NormalTok{,        }\CommentTok{\# 10 fold cross{-}validaton}
  \AttributeTok{number =} \DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{,           }
  \AttributeTok{classProbs =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{,    }\CommentTok{\# needed for multiclass AUC etc.}
  \AttributeTok{summaryFunction =}\NormalTok{ multiClassSummary,}
  \AttributeTok{verboseIter =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# train XGBoost model}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{605794011}\NormalTok{)}
\FunctionTok{invisible}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{capture.output}\NormalTok{(\{}
  \FunctionTok{suppressMessages}\NormalTok{(\{}
    \FunctionTok{suppressWarnings}\NormalTok{(\{}
\NormalTok{      xgb\_model }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{train}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{        Reason }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ .,}
        \AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ train\_data,}
        \AttributeTok{method =} \StringTok{"xgbTree"}\NormalTok{,}
        \AttributeTok{trControl =}\NormalTok{ ctrl,}
        \AttributeTok{tuneLength =} \DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{,       }\CommentTok{\# tries 5 different combinations of params, trains 10 models per set of params, 10 x 5 = 50 models total}
        \AttributeTok{metric =} \StringTok{"Accuracy"}
\NormalTok{      )}
\NormalTok{    \})}
\NormalTok{  \})}
\NormalTok{\}))}

\CommentTok{\# print model summary and best tuning parameters}
\FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(xgb\_model)}
\end{Highlighting}
